The codebase had inconsistent error handling with String-based errors, `anyhow::Error`, custom error structs, and various domain-specific error enums scattered across 85+ module files.\n\n## Key Files Identified\n\n### Files with Error Handling Patterns (Representative Sample)\n\n- `/app/project/src/module_43.txt` - Contains `RepositoryError`, `CacheError`, `ServiceError` enums with thiserror\n- `/app/project/src/module_8.txt` - Has `PageError`, `RepositoryError`, and `ServiceError` with anyhow conversions\n- `/app/project/src/module_52.txt` - Defines `ServiceError` with sqlx and redis error wrapping\n- `/app/project/src/module_71.txt` - Multiple error types: `ValidationError`, `RepoError`, `CacheError`, `ServiceError`\n- `/app/project/src/module_1.txt` - Uses `ServiceError` with actix-web `ResponseError`\n- `/app/project/src/module_2.txt` - Contains `RepositoryError` and `ServiceError` with String-based messages\n- `/app/project/src/module_3.txt` - Has HttpResponse::build(self.status_code()).json(serde_json::json!({\n            \"error\": self.to_string()\n        }))\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Identified Error Handling Patterns\n\nThe codebase analysis revealed **five distinct error handling patterns** that need consolidation:\n\n1. **Module-Local Error Enums** (most common): Each module defines its own `ServiceError`, `RepositoryError`, `CacheError` using `thiserror`. These are well-structured but duplicated across files.\n\n2. **String-Based Errors**: Some modules use `String` messages in error variants (e.g., `QueryFailed(String)`, `Internal(String)`), losing type information.\n\n3. **anyhow::Error Wrapping**: Several modules wrap errors in `anyhow::Error` for flexibility but lose specific error variant information.\n\n4. **Framework-Specific ResponseError**: Modules using Actix-web or Axum implement `ResponseError` or `IntoResponse` locally with inconsistent JSON response formats.\n\n5. **Validation Errors**: Multiple approaches to validation errors - some wrap `validator::ValidationErrors`, others use String messages.\n\n### Error Categories Discovered\n\n| Category | Source Types | HTTP Status | Frequency |\n|----------|-------------|-------------|-----------|\n| Database | `sqlx::Error`, `tokio_postgres::Error` | 500 | High |\n| Cache | `redis::RedisError` | 500 | High |\n| Validation | `validator::ValidationErrors`, `String` | 400 | High |\n| Not Found | Custom variants | 404 | Medium |\n| Authentication | Custom variants | 401 | Low |\n| Authorization | Custom variants | 403 | Low |\n| Serialization | `serde_json::Error` | 500 | Medium |\n| Internal | `anyhow::Error`, `String` | 500 | High |\n| Pagination | Custom variants | 400 | Medium |\n\n## Implementation\n\n### New File: `src/error.rs` (or `src/error.txt`)\n\nThe unified `AppError` enum should be created with the following structure:\n\n```rust\n//! src/error.rs\n//!\n//! Unified Application Error Type for LedgerLink Nexus\n//!\n//! This module provides a centralized error handling mechanism for the entire\n//! application, consolidating disparate error patterns into a single, robust type.\n\nuse axum::{\n    http::StatusCode,\n    response::{IntoResponse, Response},\n    Json,\n};\nuse serde::Serialize;\nuse thiserror::Error;\n\n/// Unified application error type representing all failure modes.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum AppError {\n    /// Validation errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Validation Error: {0}\")]\n    ValidationError(String),\n\n    /// Resource not found (HTTP 404)\n    #[error(\"Resource Not Found: {0}\")]\n    NotFound(String),\n\n    /// Authentication failure (HTTP 401)\n    #[error(\"Authentication Failed\")]\n    Unauthorized,\n\n    /// Authorization failure (HTTP 403)\n    #[error(\"Access Denied: {0}\")]\n    Forbidden(String),\n\n    /// Database errors from sqlx (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Database Error: {0}\")]\n    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    /// Cache errors from Redis (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Cache Error: {0}\")]\n    Cache(#[from] redis::RedisError),\n\n    /// Serialization errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Serialization Error: {0}\")]\n    Serialization(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n\n    /// Pagination errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Pagination Error: {0}\")]\n    PaginationError(String),\n\n    /// Repository errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Repository Error: {0}\")]\n    Repository(String),\n\n    /// Internal server errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Internal Server Error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n\n    /// Backward-compatible anyhow wrapper (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Internal Error: {0}\")]\n    Anyhow(#[from] anyhow::Error),\n\n    /// Validator crate errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Validation Error: {0}\")]\n    ValidatorError(#[from] validator::ValidationErrors),\n\n    /// Timeout errors (HTTP 504)\n    #[error(\"Operation Timeout: {0}\")]\n    Timeout(String),\n\n    /// Rate limit exceeded (HTTP 429)\n    #[error(\"Rate Limit Exceeded: {0}\")]\n    RateLimitExceeded(String),\n\n    /// Service unavailable (HTTP 503)\n    #[error(\"Service Unavailable: {0}\")]\n    ServiceUnavailable(String),\n}\n\n/// Structured JSON error response body\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct ErrorResponse {\n    pub error: ErrorDetail,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct ErrorDetail {\n    #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n    pub error_type: String,\n    pub message: String,\n}\n\nimpl AppError {\n    pub fn status_code(&self) -> StatusCode {\n        match self {\n            AppError::ValidationError(_) | AppError::PaginationError(_) |\n            AppError::ValidatorError(_) => StatusCode::BAD_REQUEST,\n            AppError::NotFound(_) => StatusCode::NOT_FOUND,\n            AppError::Unauthorized => StatusCode::UNAUTHORIZED,\n            AppError::Forbidden(_) => StatusCode::FORBIDDEN,\n            AppError::Database(_) | AppError::Cache(_) | AppError::Serialization(_) |\n            AppError::Repository(_) | AppError::Internal(_) | AppError::Anyhow(_) =>\n                StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,\n            AppError::Timeout(_) => StatusCode::GATEWAY_TIMEOUT,\n            AppError::RateLimitExceeded(_) => StatusCode::TOO_MANY_REQUESTS,\n            AppError::ServiceUnavailable(_) => StatusCode::SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn error_type(&self) -> &'static str {\n        match self {\n            AppError::ValidationError(_) | AppError::ValidatorError(_) => \"validation\",\n            AppError::NotFound(_) => \"not_found\",\n            AppError::Unauthorized => \"unauthorized\",\n            AppError::Forbidden(_) => \"forbidden\",\n            AppError::Database(_) => \"database\",\n            AppError::Cache(_) => \"cache\",\n            AppError::Serialization(_) => \"serialization\",\n            AppError::PaginationError(_) => \"pagination\",\n            AppError::Repository(_) | AppError::Internal(_) | AppError::Anyhow(_) => \"internal\",\n            AppError::Timeout(_) => \"timeout\",\n            AppError::RateLimitExceeded(_) => \"rate_limit\",\n            AppError::ServiceUnavailable(_) => \"service_unavailable\",\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl IntoResponse for AppError {\n    fn into_response(self) -> Response {\n        let status = self.status_code();\n        let body = Json(ErrorResponse {\n            error: ErrorDetail {\n                error_type: self.error_type().to_string(),\n                message: self.to_string(),\n            },\n        });\n        (status, body).into_response()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Type alias for Results using AppError\npub type AppResult<T> = Result<T, AppError>;\n\n// From implementations for common types\nimpl From<String> for AppError {\n    fn from(s: String) -> Self { AppError::Internal(s) }\n}\n\nimpl From<&str> for AppError {\n    fn from(s: &str) -> Self { AppError::Internal(s.to_string()) }\n}\n\nimpl From<tokio_postgres::Error> for AppError {\n    fn from(err: tokio_postgres::Error) -> Self { AppError::Repository(err.to_string()) }\n}\n\n// Helper constructors\nimpl AppError {\n    pub fn validation<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::ValidationError(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn not_found<S: Into<String>>(resource: S) -> Self { AppError::NotFound(resource.into()) }\n    pub fn repository<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::Repository(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn internal<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::Internal(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn pagination<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::PaginationError(msg.into()) }\n}\n```\n\n### Module Refactoring Examples\n\n#### Example 1: Refactoring module_43.txt\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\npub enum RepositoryError {\n LedgerEntryRepository: Send + Sync {\n    async fn count_entries(\n        &self,\n        tenant_id: Uuid,\n        filter: &LedgerEntryPageRequest,\n    ) -> Result<i64, RepositoryError>;\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::AppError;\n\n#[async_trait]\npub trait LedgerEntryRepository: Send + Sync {\n    async fn count_entries(\n        &self,\n        tenant_id: Uuid,\n        filter: &LedgerEntryPageRequest,\n    ) -> Result<i64, AppError>;\n}\n```\n\n#### Example 2: Refactoring module_52.txt\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub Repository(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n    #[error(\"cache error: {0}\")]\n    Cache(#[from] redis::RedisError),\n    #[error(\"unknown error: {0}\")]\n    Unknown(String),\n}\n\npub async fn ServiceError::Validation(e.to_string()))?\n        // ...\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::{AppError, AppResult};\n\npub async fn get_paginated(\n    &self,\n    raw_query: codebase analysis revealed **five distinct error handling patterns** that need consolidation:\n\n1. **Module-Local Error Enums** (most common): Each module defines its own `ServiceError`, `RepositoryError`, `CacheError` using `thiserror`. These are well-structured but duplicated across files.\n\n2. **String-Based Errors**: Some modules use `String` messages in error variants (e.g., `QueryFailed(String)`, `Internal(String)`), losing type information.\n\n3. **anyhow::Error Wrapping**: Several modules wrap errors in `anyhow::Error` for flexibility but lose specific error variant information.\n\n4. **Framework-Specific ResponseError**: Modules using Actix-web or Axum implement `ResponseError` or `IntoResponse` locally with inconsistent JSON response formats.\n\n5. **Validation Errors**: Multiple approaches to validation errors - some wrap `validator::ValidationErrors`, others use String messages.\n\n### Error Categories Discovered\n\n| Category | Source Types | HTTP Status | Frequency |\n|----------|-------------|-------------|-----------|\n| Database | `sqlx::Error`, `tokio_postgres::Error` | 500 | High |\n| Cache | `redis::RedisError` | 500 | High |\n| Validation | `validator::ValidationErrors`, `String` | 400 | High |\n| Not Found | Custom variants | 404 | Medium |\n| Authentication | Custom variants | 401 | Low |\n| Authorization | Custom variants | 403 | Low |\n| Serialization | `serde_json::Error` | 500 | Medium |\n| Internal | `anyhow::Error`, `String` | 500 | High |\n| Pagination | Custom variants | 400 | Medium |\n\n## Implementation\n\n### New File: `src/error.rs` (or `src/error.txt`)\n\nThe unified `AppError` enum should be created with the following structure:\n\n```rust\n//! src/error.rs\n//!\n//! Unified Application Error Type for LedgerLink Nexus\n//!\n//! This module provides a centralized error handling mechanism for the entire\n//! application, consolidating disparate error patterns into a single, robust type.\n\nuse axum::{\n    http::StatusCode,\n    response::{IntoResponse, Response},\n    Json,\n};\nuse serde::Serialize;\nuse thiserror::Error;\n\n/// Unified application error type representing all failure modes.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum AppError {\n    /// Validation errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Validation Error: {0}\")]\n    ValidationError(String),\n\n    /// Resource not found (HTTP 404)\n    #[error(\"Resource Not Found: {0}\")]\n    NotFound(String),\n\n    /// Authentication failure (HTTP 401)\n    #[error(\"Authentication Failed\")]\n    Unauthorized,\n\n    /// Authorization failure (HTTP 403)\n    #[error(\"Access Denied: {0}\")]\n    Forbidden(String),\n\n    /// Database errors from sqlx (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Database Error: {0}\")]\n    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    /// Cache errors from Redis (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Cache Error: {0}\")]\n    Cache(#[from] redis::RedisError),\n\n    /// Serialization errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Serialization Error: {0}\")]\n    Serialization(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n\n    /// Pagination errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Pagination Error: {0}\")]\n    PaginationError(String),\n\n    /// Repository errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Repository Error: {0}\")]\n    Repository(String),\n\n    /// Internal server errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Internal Server Error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n\n    /// Backward-compatible anyhow wrapper (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Internal Error: {0}\")]\n    Anyhow(#[from] anyhow::Error),\n\n    /// Validator crate errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Validation Error: {0}\")]\n    ValidatorError(#[from] validator::ValidationErrors),\n\n    /// Timeout errors (HTTP 504)\n    #[error(\"Operation Timeout: {0}\")]\n    Timeout(String),\n\n    /// Rate limit exceeded (HTTP 429)\n    #[error(\"Rate Limit Exceeded: {0}\")]\n    RateLimitExceeded(String),\n\n    /// Service unavailable (HTTP 503)\n    #[error(\"Service Unavailable: {0}\")]\n    ServiceUnavailable(String),\n}\n\n/// Structured JSON error response body\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct ErrorResponse {\n    pub error: ErrorDetail,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct ErrorDetail {\n    #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n    pub error_type: String,\n    pub message: String,\n}\n\nimpl AppError {\n    pub fn status_code(&self) -> StatusCode {\n        match self {\n            AppError::ValidationError(_) | AppError::PaginationError(_) |\n            AppError::ValidatorError(_) => StatusCode::BAD_REQUEST,\n            AppError::NotFound(_) => StatusCode::NOT_FOUND,\n            AppError::Unauthorized => StatusCode::UNAUTHORIZED,\n            AppError::Forbidden(_) => StatusCode::FORBIDDEN,\n            AppError::Database(_) | AppError::Cache(_) | AppError::Serialization(_) |\n            AppError::Repository(_) | AppError::Internal(_) | AppError::Anyhow(_) =>\n                StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,\n            AppError::Timeout(_) => StatusCode::GATEWAY_TIMEOUT,\n            AppError::RateLimitExceeded(_) => StatusCode::TOO_MANY_REQUESTS,\n            AppError::ServiceUnavailable(_) => StatusCode::SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn error_type(&self) -> &'static str {\n        match self {\n            AppError::ValidationError(_) | AppError::ValidatorError(_) => \"validation\",\n            AppError::NotFound(_) => \"not_found\",\n            AppError::Unauthorized => \"unauthorized\",\n            AppError::Forbidden(_) => \"forbidden\",\n            AppError::Database(_) => \"database\",\n            AppError::Cache(_) => \"cache\",\n            AppError::Serialization(_) => \"serialization\",\n            AppError::PaginationError(_) => \"pagination\",\n            AppError::Repository(_) | AppError::Internal(_) | AppError::Anyhow(_) => \"internal\",\n            AppError::Timeout(_) => \"timeout\",\n            AppError::RateLimitExceeded(_) => \"rate_limit\",\n            AppError::ServiceUnavailable(_) => \"service_unavailable\",\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl IntoResponse for AppError {\n    fn into_response(self) -> Response {\n        let status = self.status_code();\n        let body = Json(ErrorResponse {\n            error: ErrorDetail {\n                error_type: self.error_type().to_string(),\n                message: self.to_string(),\n            },\n        });\n        (status, body).into_response()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Type alias for Results using AppError\npub type AppResult<T> = Result<T, AppError>;\n\n// From implementations for common types\nimpl From<String> for AppError {\n    fn from(s: String) -> Self { AppError::Internal(s) }\n}\n\nimpl From<&str> for AppError {\n    fn from(s: &str) -> Self { AppError::Internal(s.to_string()) }\n}\n\nimpl From<tokio_postgres::Error> for AppError {\n    fn from(err: tokio_postgres::Error) -> Self { AppError::Repository(err.to_string()) }\n}\n\n// Helper constructors\nimpl AppError {\n    pub fn validation<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::ValidationError(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn not_found<S: Into<String>>(resource: S) -> Self { AppError::NotFound(resource.into()) }\n    pub fn repository<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::Repository(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn internal<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::Internal(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn pagination<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::PaginationError(msg.into()) }\n}\n```\n\n### Module Refactoring Examples\n\n#### Example 1: Refactoring module_43.txt\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\npub enum RepositoryError {\n    #[error(\"database error: {0}\")]\n    Db(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n    #[error(\"unknown repository error: {0}\")]\n    Other(#[from] anyhow::Error),\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\npub trait LedgerEntryRepository: Send + Sync {\n    async fn count_entries(\n        &self,\n        tenant_id: Uuid,\n        filter: &LedgerEntryPageRequest,\n    ) -> Result<i64, RepositoryError>;\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::AppError;\n\n#[async_trait]\npub trait LedgerEntryRepository: Send + Sync {\n    async fn count_entries(\n        &self,\n        tenant_id: Uuid,\n        filter: &LedgerEntryPageRequest,\n    ) -> Result<i64, AppError>;\n}\n```\n\n#### Example 2: Refactoring module_52.txt\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum ServiceError {\n    #[error(\"validation failed: {0}\")]\n    Validation(String),\n    #[error(\"resource not found\")]\n    NotFound,\n    #[error(\"repository error: {0}\")]\n    Repository(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n    #[error(\"cache error: {0}\")]\n    Cache(#[from] redis::RedisError),\n    #[error(\"unknown error: {0}\")]\n    Unknown(String),\n}\n\npub async fn get_paginated(\n    &self,\n    raw_query: LedgerEntryQuery,\n) -> Result<Paginated<LedgerEntryView>, ServiceError> {\n    let query = raw_query\n        .validate()\n        .map_err(|e| ServiceError::Validation(e.to_string()))?\n        // ...\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::{AppError, AppResult};\n\npub async fn get_paginated(\n    &self,\n    raw_query: LedgerEntryQuery,\n) -> AppResult<Paginated<LedgerEntryView>> {\n    let query = raw_query.validate()?;  // validator::ValidationErrors auto-converts\n    // ...\n}\n```\n\n#### Example 3: Refactoring module_3.txt with Authentication\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\npub enum LedgerEntryServiceError {\n    #[error(\"validation error: {0}\")]\n    Validation(String),\n    #[error(\"unauthorised\")]\n    Unauthorised,\n    #[error(\"not found\")]\n    NotFound,\n    #[error(\"repository error: {0}\")]\n    Repository(String),\n}\n\nif !auth.can_read_ledger() {\n    return Err(LedgerEntryServiceError::Unauthorised);\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::AppError;\n\nif !auth.can_read_ledger() {\n    return Err(AppError::Unauthorized);\n}\n```\n\n### Files to Modify\n\nAll 85 module files (`module_1.txt` through `module_85.txt`) plus utility files need modification:\n\n| File Pattern | Changes Required |\n|--------------|-----------------|\n| `src/module_*.txt` | Remove local error enums, add `use crate::error::AppError;`, change return types to `Result<T, AppError>` |\n| `src/utils.txt` | Update error handling to use `AppError` |\n| `src/config.txt` | If error handling exists, update to use `AppError` |\n\n### Error Variant Mapping\n\n| Old Error Type | New AppError Variant |\n|---------------|---------------------|\n| `RepositoryError::Db(sqlx::Error)` | `AppError::Database` (auto via From) |\n| `CacheError::Redis(redis::RedisError)` | `AppError::Cache` (auto via From) |\n| `ServiceError::Validation(String)` | failed (status: {status}) \u2013 body: {body}\")\n    })\n}\n```\n\n**After (with error response handling):**\n```rust\n/// Structured error response from the API\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\npub message: String,\n}\n\n/// Parse a successful JSON response\npub async fn json<T>(resp: Response) -> Result<T>\nwhere\n    T: DeserializeOwned,\n{\n    // existing implementation\n}\n\n/// Assert that a response is an error with the expected type and status\npub async fn assert_error_response(\n    resp: Response,\n    expected_status: StatusCode,\n    expected_type: &str,\n) -> Result<ApiErrorResponse> {\n    assert_eq!(resp.status(), expected_status, \"Unexpected HTTP status\");\n\n    let bytes = resp.bytes().await.context(\"Reading error response body\")?;\n    let error_resp: ApiErrorResponse = serde_json::from_slice(&bytes)\n        .context(\"Decoding error JSON\")?;\n\n    assert_eq!(\n        error_resp.error.error_type, expected_type,\n        \"Unexpected error type\"\n    );\n\n    Ok(error_resp)\n}\n\n/// Example test using the new assertion\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn test_validation_error_returns_400() -> Result<()> {\n    let app = spawn_app().await;\n\n    // Send request with invalid pagination\n    let resp = app.get(\"/v1/ledger-entries?page=0&per_page=-1\").await;\n\n    // Assert structured error response\n    let error = The codebase had inconsistent error handling with String-based errors, `anyhow::Error`, custom error structs, and various domain-specific error enums scattered across 85+ module files.\n\n## Key Files anyhow::Error),\n}\n\nimpl ResponseError for ApiError {\n    fn status_code(&self) -> StatusCode {\n        match self {\n            ApiError::Validation(_) => StatusCode::BAD_REQUEST,\n            ApiError::Anyhow(_) => StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn error_response(&self) -> HttpResponse {\n        HttpResponse::build(self.status_code()).json(serde_json::json!({\n            \"error\": self.to_string()\n        }))\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Identified Error Handling Patterns\n\nThe codebase analysis revealed **five distinct error handling patterns** that need consolidation:\n\n1. **Module-Local Error Enums** (most common): Each module defines its own `ServiceError`, `RepositoryError`, `CacheError` using `thiserror`. These are well-structured but duplicated across files.\n\n2. **String-Based Errors**: Some modules use `String` messages in error variants (e.g., `QueryFailed(String)`, `Internal(String)`), losing type information.\n\n3. **anyhow::Error Wrapping**: Several modules wrap errors in `anyhow::Error` for flexibility but lose specific error variant information.\n\n4. **Framework-Specific ResponseError**: Modules using Actix-web or Axum implement `ResponseError` or `IntoResponse` locally with inconsistent JSON response formats.\n\n5. **Validation Errors**: Multiple approaches to validation errors - some wrap `validator::ValidationErrors`, others use String messages.\n\n### Error Categories Discovered\n\n| Category | Source Types | HTTP Status | Frequency |\n|----------|-------------|-------------|-----------|\n| Database | `sqlx::Error`, `tokio_postgres::Error` | 500 | High |\n| Cache | `redis::RedisError` | 500 | High |\n| Validation | `validator::ValidationErrors`, `String` | 400 | High |\n| Not Found | Custom variants | 404 | Medium |\n| Authentication | Custom variants | 401 | Low |\n| Authorization | Custom variants | 403 | Low |\n| Serialization | `serde_json::Error` | 500 | Medium |\n| Internal | `anyhow::Error`, `String` | 500 | High |\n| Pagination | Custom variants | 400 | Medium |\n\n## Implementation\n\n### New File: `src/error.rs` (or `src/error.txt`)\n\nThe unified `AppError` enum should be created with the following structure:\n\n```rust\n//! src/error.rs\n//!\n//! Unified Application Error Type for LedgerLink Nexus\n//!\n//! This module provides a centralized error handling mechanism for the entire\n//! application, consolidating disparate error patterns into a single, robust type.\n\nuse axum::{\n    http::StatusCode,\n    response::{IntoResponse, Response},\n    Json,\n};\nuse serde::Serialize;\nuse thiserror::Error;\n\n/// Unified application error type representing all failure modes.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum AppError {\n    /// Validation errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Validation Error: {0}\")]\n    ValidationError(String),\n\n    /// Resource not found (HTTP 404)\n    #[error(\"Resource Not Found: {0}\")]\n    NotFound(String),\n\n    /// Authentication failure (HTTP 401)\n    #[error(\"Authentication Failed\")]\n    Unauthorized,\n\n    /// Authorization failure (HTTP 403)\n    #[error(\"Access Denied: {0}\")]\n    Forbidden(String),\n\n    /// Database errors from sqlx (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Database Error: {0}\")]\n    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    /// Cache errors from Redis (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Cache Error: {0}\")]\n    Cache(#[from] redis::RedisError),\n\n    /// Serialization errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Serialization Error: {0}\")]\n    Serialization(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n\n    /// Pagination errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Pagination Error: {0}\")]\n    PaginationError(String),\n\n    /// Repository errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Repository Error: {0}\")]\n    Repository(String),\n\n    /// Internal server errors (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Internal Server Error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n\n    /// Backward-compatible anyhow wrapper (HTTP 500)\n    #[error(\"Internal Error: {0}\")]\n    Anyhow(#[from] anyhow::Error),\n\n    /// Validator crate errors (HTTP 400)\n    #[error(\"Validation Error: {0}\")]\n    ValidatorError(#[from] validator::ValidationErrors),\n\n    /// Timeout errors (HTTP 504)\n    #[error(\"Operation Timeout: {0}\")]\n    Timeout(String),\n\n    /// Rate limit exceeded (HTTP 429)\n    #[error(\"Rate Limit Exceeded: {0}\")]\n    RateLimitExceeded(String),\n\n    /// Service unavailable (HTTP 503)\n    #[error(\"Service Unavailable: {0}\")]\n    ServiceUnavailable(String),\n}\n\n/// Structured JSON error response body\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct ErrorResponse {\n    pub error: ErrorDetail,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\npub struct ErrorDetail {\n    #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n    pub error_type: String,\n    pub message: String,\n}\n\nimpl AppError {\n    pub fn status_code(&self) -> StatusCode {\n        match self {\n            AppError::ValidationError(_) | AppError::PaginationError(_) |\n            AppError::ValidatorError(_) => StatusCode::BAD_REQUEST,\n            AppError::NotFound(_) => StatusCode::NOT_FOUND,\n            AppError::Unauthorized => StatusCode::UNAUTHORIZED,\n            AppError::Forbidden(_) => StatusCode::FORBIDDEN,\n            AppError::Database(_) | AppError::Cache(_) | AppError::Serialization(_) |\n            AppError::Repository(_) | AppError::Internal(_) | AppError::Anyhow(_) =>\n                StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,\n            AppError::Timeout(_) => StatusCode::GATEWAY_TIMEOUT,\n            AppError::RateLimitExceeded(_) => StatusCode::TOO_MANY_REQUESTS,\n            AppError::ServiceUnavailable(_) => StatusCode::SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn error_type(&self) -> &'static str {\n        match self {\n            AppError::ValidationError(_) | AppError::ValidatorError(_) => \"validation\",\n            AppError::NotFound(_) => \"not_found\",\n            AppError::Unauthorized => \"unauthorized\",\n            AppError::Forbidden(_) => \"forbidden\",\n            AppError::Database(_) => \"database\",\n            AppError::Cache(_) => \"cache\",\n            AppError::Serialization(_) => \"serialization\",\n            AppError::PaginationError(_) => \"pagination\",\n            AppError::Repository(_) | AppError::Internal(_) | AppError::Anyhow(_) => \"internal\",\n            AppError::Timeout(_) => \"timeout\",\n            AppError::RateLimitExceeded(_) => \"rate_limit\",\n            AppError::ServiceUnavailable(_) => \"service_unavailable\",\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl IntoResponse for AppError {\n    fn into_response(self) -> Response {\n        let status = self.status_code();\n        let body = Json(ErrorResponse {\n            error: ErrorDetail {\n                error_type: self.error_type().to_string(),\n                message: self.to_string(),\n            },\n        });\n        (status, body).into_response()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Type alias for Results using AppError\npub type AppResult<T> = Result<T, AppError>;\n\n// From implementations for common types\nimpl From<String> for AppError {\n    fn from(s: String) -> Self { AppError::Internal(s) }\n}\n\nimpl From<&str> for AppError {\n    fn from(s: &str) -> Self { AppError::Internal(s.to_string()) }\n}\n\nimpl From<tokio_postgres::Error> for AppError {\n    fn from(err: tokio_postgres::Error) -> Self { AppError::Repository(err.to_string()) }\n}\n\n// Helper constructors\nimpl AppError {\n    pub fn validation<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::ValidationError(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn not_found<S: Into<String>>(resource: S) -> Self { AppError::NotFound(resource.into()) }\n    pub fn repository<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::Repository(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn internal<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::Internal(msg.into()) }\n    pub fn pagination<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self { AppError::PaginationError(msg.into()) }\n}\n```\n\n### Module Refactoring Examples\n\n#### Example 1: Refactoring module_43.txt\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\npub enum RepositoryError {\n    #[error(\"database error: {0}\")]\n    Db(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n    #[error(\"unknown repository error: {0}\")]\n    Other(#[from] anyhow::Error),\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\npub trait LedgerEntryRepository: Send + Sync {\n    async fn count_entries(\n        &self,\n        tenant_id: Uuid,\n        filter: &LedgerEntryPageRequest,\n    ) -> Result<i64, RepositoryError>;\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::AppError;\n\n#[async_trait]\npub trait LedgerEntryRepository: Send + Sync {\n    async fn count_entries(\n        &self,\n        tenant_id: Uuid,\n        filter: &LedgerEntryPageRequest,\n    ) -> Result<i64, AppError>;\n}\n```\n\n#### Example 2: Refactoring module_52.txt\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum ServiceError {\n    #[error(\"validation failed: {0}\")]\n    Validation(String),\n    #[error(\"resource not found\")]\n    NotFound,\n    #[error(\"repository error: {0}\")]\n    Repository(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n    #[error(\"cache error: {0}\")]\n    Cache(#[from] redis::RedisError),\n    #[error(\"unknown error: {0}\")]\n    Unknown(String),\n}\n\npub async fn get_paginated(\n    &self,\n    raw_query: LedgerEntryQuery,\n) -> Result<Paginated<LedgerEntryView>, ServiceError> {\n    let query = raw_query\n        .validate()\n        .map_err(|e| ServiceError::Validation(e.to_string()))?\n        // ...\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::{AppError, AppResult};\n\npub async fn get_paginated(\n    &self,\n    raw_query: LedgerEntryQuery,\n) -> AppResult<Paginated<LedgerEntryView>> {\n    let query = raw_query.validate()?;  // validator::ValidationErrors auto-converts\n    // ...\n}\n```\n\n#### Example 3: Refactoring module_3.txt with Authentication\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\npub enum LedgerEntryServiceError {\n    #[error(\"validation error: {0}\")]\n    Validation(String),\n    #[error(\"unauthorised\")]\n    Unauthorised,\n    #[error(\"not found\")]\n    NotFound,\n    #[error(\"repository error: {0}\")]\n    Repository(String),\n}\n\nif !auth.can_read_ledger() {\n    return Err(LedgerEntryServiceError::Unauthorised);\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```rust\nuse crate::error::AppError;\n\nif !auth.can_read_ledger() {\n    return Err(AppError::Unauthorized);\n}\n```\n\n### Files to Modify\n\nAll 85 module files (`module_1.txt` through `module_85.txt`) plus utility files need modification:\n\n| File Pattern | Changes Required |\n|--------------|-----------------|\n| `src/module_*.txt` | Remove local error enums, add `use crate::error::AppError;`, change return types to `Result<T, AppError>` |\n| `src/utils.txt` | Update error handling to use `AppError` |\n| `src/config.txt` | If error handling exists, update to use `AppError` |\n\n### Error Variant Mapping\n\n| Old Error Type | New AppError Variant |\n|---------------|---------------------|\n| `RepositoryError::Db(sqlx::Error)` | `AppError::Database` (auto via From) |\n| `CacheError::Redis(redis::RedisError)` | `AppError::Cache` (auto via From) |\n| `ServiceError::Validation(String)` | `AppError::ValidationError(String)` |\n| `ServiceError::NotFound` | `AppError::NotFound(String)` |\n| `LedgerEntryServiceError::Unauthorised` | `AppError::Unauthorized` |\n| `RepositoryError::Other(anyhow::Error)` | `AppError::Anyhow` (auto via From) |\n| `ServiceError::Internal(String)` | `AppError::Internal(String)` |\n| `PageError::InvalidLimit(u32)` | `AppError::PaginationError(String)` |\n\n### Test Modifications for `tests/test_utils.txt`\n\nTo validate the new structured JSON error responses, the test utilities should be updated:\n\n**Before:**\n```rust\npub async fn json<T>(resp: Response) -> Result<T>\nwhere\n    T: DeserializeOwned,\n{\n    let status = resp.status();\n    let bytes = resp.bytes().await.context(\"Reading response body\")?;\n    serde_json::from_slice(&bytes).with_context(|| {\n        let body = String::from_utf8_lossy(&bytes);\n        format!(\"Decoding JSON failed (status: {status}) \u2013 body: {body}\")\n    })\n}\n```\n\n**After (with error response handling):**\n```rust\n/// Structured error response from the API\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\npub struct ApiErrorResponse {\n    pub error: ApiErrorDetail,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\npub struct ApiErrorDetail {\n    #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n    pub error_type: String,\n    pub message: String,\n}\n\n/// Parse a successful JSON response\npub async fn json<T>(resp: Response) -> Result<T>\nwhere\n    T: DeserializeOwned,\n{\n    // existing implementation\n}\n\n/// Assert that a response is an error with the expected type and status\npub async fn assert_error_response(\n    resp: Response,\n    expected_status: StatusCode,\n    expected_type: &str,\n) -> Result<ApiErrorResponse> {\n    assert_eq!(resp.status(), expected_status, \"Unexpected HTTP status\");\n\n    let bytes = resp.bytes().await.context(\"Reading error response body\")?;\n    let error_resp: ApiErrorResponse = serde_json::from_slice(&bytes)\n        .context(\"Decoding error JSON\")?;\n\n    assert_eq!(\n        error_resp.error.error_type, expected_type,\n        \"Unexpected error type\"\n    );\n\n    Ok(error_resp)\n}\n\n/// Example test using the new assertion\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn test_validation_error_returns_400() -> Result<()> {\n    let app = spawn_app().await;\n\n    // Send request with invalid pagination\n    let resp = app.get(\"/v1/ledger-entries?page=0&per_page=-1\").await;\n\n    // Assert structured error response\n    let error = Ok(())\n}\n\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn test_not_found_returns_404() -> Result<()> {\n    let app = spawn_app().await;\n    let token = bearer_token(Uuid::new_v4(), &[\"finance.read\"])?;\n\n    let resp = app\n        .http_client\n        .get(app.url(\"/v1/nonexistent-resource/12345\"))\n        .bearer(&token)\n        .send()\n        .await?;\n\n    let error = assert_error_response(\n        resp,\n        StatusCode::NOT_FOUND,\n        \"not_found\"\n    ).await?;\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn test_unauthorized_returns_401() -> Result<()> {\n    let app = |\n|---------|-------------|----------|\n| `ValidationError` | 400 | Invalid input data |\n| `NotFound` | 404 | Resource doesn't exist |\n| `Unauthorized` | 401 | Missing/invalid authentication |\n| pagination params |\n| `Repository` | 500 | Generic data access errors |\n| `Internal` | 500 | Unexpected conditions |\n| `Anyhow` | 500 | Backward compatibility |\n| `ValidatorError` | 400 | validator crate errors |\n| `Timeout` | 504 | Operation timeouts |\n| `RateLimitExceeded` | 429 | Rate limiting |\n| `ServiceUnavailable` | 503 | Service degradation |\n\n### Recommendations\n\n1. **Incremental Rollout**: Start by refactoring one module (e.g., `module_8.txt`) completely, then apply the pattern systematically to remaining modules.\n\n2. **Feature Flag**: Consider a feature flag during migration to toggle between old and new error handling.\n\n3. **Metrics Integration**: Add metrics emission in the `IntoResponse` implementation to track error frequency by type.\n\n4. **Error Logging**: Enhance with `tracing` integration to log errors with appropriate severity levels.\n\n5. **API Documentation**: Update OpenAPI/Swagger specs to reflect the new consistent error response format.\n",

```rust
//! src/error.rs
//!
//! Unified Application Error Type for LedgerLink Nexus
//!
//! This module provides a centralized error handling mechanism for the entire
//! application. It consolidates the various error handling patterns that were
//! previously scattered across different modules (String errors, anyhow::Error,
//! custom error structs) into a single, robust, and expressive AppError type.
//!
//! Key Features:
//! - Implements std::error::Error and std::fmt::Display via thiserror
//! - Provides From<T> conversions for common error types (sqlx, redis, etc.)
//! - Implements axum::response::IntoResponse for HTTP error responses
//! - Maps each variant to appropriate HTTP status codes
//! - Returns consistent JSON error envelopes

use axum::{
    http::StatusCode,
    response::{IntoResponse, Response},
    Json,
};
use serde::Serialize;
use serde_json::json;
use thiserror::Error;

/// Unified application error type that represents all failure modes in
/// the LedgerLink Nexus microservice.
///
/// This enum consolidates error handling across the entire application,
/// providing consistent error responses and appropriate HTTP status codes.
#[derive(Debug, Error)]
pub enum AppError {
    /// Validation errors for invalid user input or request parameters.
    /// Maps to HTTP 400 Bad Request.
    #[error("Validation Error: {0}")]
    ValidationError(String),

    /// Resource not found errors.
    /// Maps to HTTP 404 Not Found.
    #[error("Resource Not Found: {0}")]
    NotFound(String),

    /// Authentication failures - user is not authenticated.
    /// Maps to HTTP 401 Unauthorized.
    #[error("Authentication Failed")]
    Unauthorized,

    /// Authorization failures - user lacks required permissions.
    /// Maps to HTTP 403 Forbidden.
    #[error("A
... (truncated)

3. WRITE /logs/agent/solution.md
# Solution: rust_api_microservice_expert_008_cross_file_refactoring_expert_01

## Task Summary

This task required consolidating disparate error handling patterns across the LedgerLink Nexus microservice into a unified `AppError` type in a new `src/error.rs` file. The codebase had inconsistent error handling with String-based errors, `anyhow::Error`, custom error structs, and various domain-specific error enums scattered across 85+ module files.

## Key Files Identified

### Files with Error Handling Patterns (Representative Sample)

- `/app/project/src/module_43.txt` - Contains `RepositoryError`, `CacheError`, `ServiceError` enums with thiserror
- `/app/project/src/module_8.txt` - Has `PageError`, `RepositoryError`, and `ServiceError` with anyhow conversions
- `/app/project/src/module_52.txt` - Defines `ServiceError` with sqlx and redis error wrapping
- `/app/project/src/module_71.txt` - Multiple error types: `ValidationError`, `RepoError`, `CacheError`, `ServiceError`
- `/app/project/src/module_1.txt` - Uses `ServiceError` with actix-web `ResponseError`
- `/app/project/src/module_2.txt` - Contains `RepositoryError` and `ServiceError` with String-based messages
- `/app/project/src/module_3.txt` - Has `LedgerEntryServiceError` with anyhow Repository wrapping
- `/app/project/src/module_10.txt` - Defines `ServiceError`, `RepositoryError`, `CacheError` with tokio_postgres
- `/app/project/src/module_20.txt` - Contains `RepoError`, `CacheError`, `ServiceError`
- `/app/project/src/module_30.txt` - Has `CacheError` with actix-web `ResponseError`
- `/app/project/src/module_40.txt` - Defines `CacheError` with anyhow wrapping
- `/app/project/src/module_50.txt` - Contains `LedgerError` with actix-web integration
- `/app/project/src/module_60.txt` - Has `ApiError` with validator an
... (truncated)
